## Session Summary
Project review full action item execution (A-01~B-04): Wave 1~3 + B-04 all complete. 7 PRs merged (#183~#189). Unicode corruption repaired in CLAUDE.md/GEMINI.md, agent registry fixed, 39 scripts @version headers added, CI npm audit added, skill triggers metadata populated, ADR frontmatter standardized, README placeholders removed, propagate-to-templates.ts newly implemented.

## Decisions
- **A-07 cancelled**: `templates/common/CLAUDE.md`/`GEMINI.md`/`CONSTITUTION.md` explicitly rejected by `validate-templates.ts` as workspace-level files — original review diagnosis was incorrect; these must NOT be in templates/common/
- **A-06 already done**: 3 skills (audit-workspace, security-scan, validate-docs-links) were already synced to templates/common/ before this session
- **list-template-versions .sh/.ps1 rejected**: Tier 2 script (bun required anyway); new-project error message updated to reference `.ts` directly
- **propagate-to-templates.ts pull-based design**: push approach rejected (risk of silent variant customization overwrite); pull with --dry-run → --apply gives explicit human control
- **propagation-map.json externalised**: non-engineers can add domains without touching script code

- **36 lifecycle-sync warnings** (non-blocking) — mostly @version headers missing in helper scripts not covered by A-05 scope
- **B-04 helpers/ exclusions** — 9 scaffolding-internal helpers excluded from propagation map; confirm exclusion list is correct with next new-project test

- **High (8)**: 32 scripts missing @version, VERSION_MANIFEST N/A entries, 3 skills L0→L1 drift, templates/common/ missing CLAUDE.md/GEMINI.md
- **Moderate (6)**: ADR formatting, placeholder READMEs, infrastructure files missing, skill triggers metadata

## Actions Required
- **Phase 1 (Critical)**: Fix mojibake, add lifecycle-manager to roster, add role: frontmatter, fix shell script drift
- **Phase 2 (High)**: Add @version to 32 scripts, sync skills to templates, create platform docs in common/
- **Phase 3 (Moderate)**: Fix ADR frontmatter, complete placeholder READMEs, add infrastructure files

- **Governance**: Excellent template contracts, robust common layer (54+ scripts), strong PM Gateway enforcement
- **Security**: Comprehensive Git hooks, gitleaks integration, minimal CI permissions
- **Documentation**: Bilingual README policy, comprehensive constitution coverage, well-maintained CHANGELOG
- **Automation**: Clean hook architecture, VERSION_MANIFEST innovation, strong scaffolding scripts

## Session Summary
2026-06-01 — Major workspace governance improvements across 10 PRs (#165~#174)

## Changes
- `templates/common/agents/auditor.md` — REMOVED from common (workspace-root-only)
- `templates/common/agents/lifecycle-manager.md` — REMOVED from common
- `templates/common/skills/` — 5 skill owners changed to `pm`; `simulate-project-creation` removed
- `templates/common/docs/context.md` — File Organization Policy, Research Standards, Computational Integrity Standards added
- `AGENTS.md` — Universal Baseline: File Organization, Source Attribution, Computational Integrity bullets added
- `skills/agent-lifecycle-manager/SKILL.md` — research/numerical/education role checklist items added
- `skills/skill-lifecycle-manager/SKILL.md` — education-purpose skill checklist item added
- `scripts/audit.ts` (v2.3.2) — root .md detection check (L2), research References WARN check added
- `scripts/new-project.sh/.ps1` — js-yaml-based parseFrontmatter fixes nested YAML (tier.antigravity bug)
- `scripts/validate-templates.ts` — common skill owner check, SKILLS_FORBIDDEN_IN_COMMON blocklist added
- `scripts/skill-lifecycle-audit.ts` — orphan owner FAIL → WARNING
- `CLAUDE.md`/`GEMINI.md` + all variants — PM boilerplate: workspace root uses specialist dispatch, variant uses pm direct; context declaration rule added
- `.claude/settings.json` — permission allowlist: 5 audit/verification commands added
- `README.md`/`README_ko.md` — agents/, skills/, tests/ added to structure diagram; .cmd→.ps1 fixed
- `docs/workspace-schema.json` — moved from root; `validate-model-registry.ts` + `validate-templates.ts` marked L0-only
- `tests/` — integration/ flattened to tests/ root; test-runner.ts path updated
- `templates/co-*/docs/` — variant-specific subdirs pre-created (.gitkeep): reports/, drafts/, research/, adr/, specs/, etc.
- `docs/templates/common-contract.json` — auditor, lifecycle-manager, simulate-project-creation entries removed

## Decisions
- **auditor/lifecycle-manager isolation**: removed from templates/common; workspace-root-only agents; variant projects use PM + lifecycle skills
- **Skill owner policy**: all common skills owner=pm (single pattern); skill-lifecycle-audit orphan→WARNING not FAIL; owner=maintainer semantics
- **PM boilerplate context rule**: workspace root → specialist dispatch (lifecycle-manager N-1, auditor N); variant → pm direct; declared above every execution plan table
- **File organization**: 3-layer enforcement (rules in context.md + pre-created structure + audit.ts detection)
- **Research Standards**: source citation mandatory for all agents (prohibition principle → universal)
- **Computational Integrity**: external tool delegation mandatory for Class A domains (prohibition principle → universal)
- **Socratic method**: role-selective methodology (not universal); only in education/tutoring/coaching agent+skill creation checklists
- **js-yaml fix**: section-merge parseFrontmatter replaced with js-yaml to preserve nested YAML (tier: antigravity/gemini-cli fields)
- **workspace-schema.json location**: moved to docs/ as it is an important governance file, not a root-level config

## Open Issues
- G-04: Future refactor — group Research + Computational Standards under `## Quality & Integrity Standards` parent section in context.md (low priority)
- `agents/pm.md` frontmatter `role:` field missing in all 8 workspace agents (pre-existing warning, not blocking)
- `co-work2` test project remains at C:/git/ root (intentional, but could be cleaned up)
